At your beginnings I immediately fell in love with you ... I did not know English well ... but with each of your songs through your instruments, your notes and the penetrating and exciting voice of Chris my soul knew perfectly what feeling they were painting, and the nice thing was that as soon as I went to read the translation of the text, a smile crossed my face because I was happy to have perceived only with their musical warmth, the feeling and the meaning of the song. Their music is universal because their music is love, and love is a language that is understandable to the whole world without distinction of language or ethnicity.
